### Note & FAQ

#### Note

* A journey's Time-Based Trigger can only have **one recurrence rule** (e.g., you cannot set a journey to trigger _both_ every Monday and on the 15th of the month).
* The system updates the target segment\*\* in the early morning on the day\*\* the journey is triggered. Users added to the segment after this update time will be included in the next run, not the current one.
* The Engagement Split node can only check the open/click status of the **immediately preceding** "Send LINE Message" node.
* The maximum number of tags that can be added or removed in a single node is 5.

#### FAQ

1. **Q: If I set a journey to run daily, can the same user enter it every day?**

* A: Yes. If the user is still in the target segment when the trigger runs, they will re-enter the journey. This is useful for daily updates but be sure your journey logic handles re-entry gracefully. If the client want to set up the upper limit of entry times to the user, please use the ‚ÄúTrigger limitation‚Äù.

2. **Q: Can this feature directly change a user's Rich Menu?**

* A: Not directly, but it's the critical first step. You use the "Add Tag" node to give a user a specific tag (e.g., "VIP"). Then, our Rich Menu system uses that "VIP" tag to automatically switch them to the VIP menu. This journey feature is the engine that enables that automated personalization.

3. **Q: Does the segment trigger include both CDH segments and AI segments?**

* A: Yes, the segment trigger supports both CDH segments and AI segments.

4. **Q: I want to ask if ‚ÄúÂàÜÁúæÊòØÊ†πÊìöÊ≠∑Âè≤Ë≥áÊñôÁî¢ÁîüÔºå‰∏¶ÊúÉÂú®Ëß∏ÁôºÊôÇÈñìÂâç 2 Â∞èÊôÇÊõ¥Êñ∞‚Äù is wrong? The segment should be updated follow by the current mechanism - Catherine**

* ![](<../../../.gitbook/assets/Unknown image (86)>)

5. **Q: Which tag that journey action of ‚ÄúAdd a tag‚Äù? - Catherine**

* MAAC Tag

6. **Q: ÊàëÂæóÁî®‰∏≠ÊñáÂïè XD ÊÉ≥ÂïèÊàëÁöÑÁêÜËß£Â∞ç‰∏çÂ∞ç„ÄåÊàëË®≠ÂÆö‰∏ÄÂÄãÊóÖÁ®ãÁÇ∫ A ÂàÜÁúæÔºåÊØèÂ§© 10:00 Ëß∏ÁôºË∑ë‰∏ÄÊ¨°ÔºåÁèæÂú®ÂàÜÁúæÊõ¥Êñ∞Ê©üÂà∂ÁÇ∫Ë∑üËëóÈöî‰∏ÄÂ§©ÊúâÊ≤íÊúâË¢´ÂÆâÊéíÊé®Êí≠ÔºåÂÅáË®≠Ê≤íÊúâÂÆâÊéíÔºåÊØèÂ§© 10:00 ÊôÇÔºåÊ≤íÊúâ‰ªª‰ΩïËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫Ë∑ëÈÄ≤‰æÜÔºõÂÅáË®≠ÊúâË¢´ÂÆâÊéíÔºå03:00-06:00 ÊôÇÔºå‰∏çÊúÉÁôºÁîü‰∫ãÊÉÖÔºå‰ΩÜ 10:00 ÊôÇÔºåÊóÖÁ®ãËß∏ÁôºÈñãÂßãË∑ëÔºåA ÂàÜÁúæÊ≤íÊúâÊõ¥Êñ∞ÂâçÁöÑ a, b ËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÂíåÊõ¥Êñ∞ÂæåÊñ∞Âä†ÂÖ•ÁöÑ c ËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÔºåÂ∞±ÊúÉË∑ëÈÄ≤‰æÜÔºåÂõ†Ê≠§ a,b,c ËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÁúüÊ≠£Ëß∏ÁôºÊóÖÁ®ãÁöÑÊôÇÈñìÔºåÊòØ 10:00Ôºå‰∏¶‰∏çÊòØÂàÜÁúæË¢´Êõ¥Êñ∞ÁöÑÊôÇÈñì„Äç- Catherine**

### Setting (For CSM)

All features are configured directly within the Journey canvas UI. No special backend settings are required for activation.

* **To Enable for a Customer:** Ensure the client‚Äôs plan includes the advanced Journey feature set.
* **Setup Guide:** For a detailed walkthrough on setting up a Rich Menu switch based on a journey tag, please refer to the CSM Advanced Playbook: \[Link to CSM Playbook Document].

### Scenario

\[not supported in journey v2.2] User Story 1: Switch Richmenu for users within their first 30 days

Setup Flow:

* Create a Richmenu configured to switch based on the tag ‚ÄúNew joiner in 30 days.‚Äù
* Create a segment named ‚ÄúNew joiner in 30 days‚Äù with a filter: Created within the past 30 days.
* Create a journey:
  * Trigger: Daily at 9:00 AM., Target Segment: ‚ÄúNew joiner in 30 days‚Äù
  * Action: Add the tag ‚ÄúNew joiner in 30 days‚Äù to trigger the Richmenu switch.

\[not supported in journey v2.2] User Story 2: Switch Richmenu for users with high purchase potential (PPP)

Setup Flow:

* Create a Richmenu configured to switch based on the tag ‚ÄúHigh Potential Buyer (PPP).‚Äù
* Create a segment named ‚ÄúHigh Potential Buyer (PPP)‚Äù based on purchase prediction logic.
* Create a journey:
  * Trigger: Every Monday at 10:00 AM., Target Segment: ‚ÄúHigh Potential Buyer (PPP).‚Äù
  * Add the tag ‚ÄúHigh Potential Buyer (PPP)‚Äù to switch the Richmenu.
  * Send a reward message (e.g., discount coupon or gift) to incentivize conversion.

A. Join LINE Event Trigger

* **User Story:** As a marketer, I want to trigger a journey the moment a user joins our LINE official account, so that I can immediately engage new followers with a welcome message, an introductory offer, or a guided onboarding experience to improve conversion and retention from the very beginning.
* **How it Works:** When a user adds the brand's LINE Official Account, MAAC receives a "follow event" from LINE. This event immediately triggers the assigned journey for that new follower.
* **Trigger Condition:** The journey is triggered by the "LINE Event - Add Friend" (Áï∂ËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫Âä†ÂÖ•Â•ΩÂèã).

B. Block LINE Event Trigger

* **User Story:** As a marketer, I want to trigger a journey the moment a user blocks our LINE official account, so that I can automatically reach out via alternative channels like email or SMS. This allows me to understand the reason for their departure through a survey, attempt to win them back with a targeted offer, or simply maintain the customer relationship on a different platform.
* **How it Works:** When a user blocks the LINE Official Account, MAAC receives an "unfollow event". This event triggers a journey for that specific user, enabling follow-up actions on other channels.
* **Trigger Condition:** The journey is triggered by the "LINE Event - Block Friend" (Áï∂ËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫Â∞ÅÈéñÂ•ΩÂèã).

## Journey v2.3

Real-Time Retargeting with SDK Events

Unlock powerful, real-time customer engagement by triggering journeys and sending personalized retargeting messages based on immediate website actions.

| PM Owner                | Lydia Hou |
| ----------------------- | --------- |
| **Product**             | MAAC      |
| **Region**              | All       |
| **Target Release Date** | TBD       |

#### Background

In our mission to empower marketers with the most responsive and effective tools, we identified a critical need to bridge the gap between real-time user behavior and automated journey activation<sup>1</sup>. While our GA4 integration provides valuable insights, the inherent data latency can delay crucial marketing responses<sup>2</sup>. Furthermore, some enterprise clients have expressed concerns about GA4 access permissions, seeking more direct control over their data sharing<sup>3</sup>.

Journey v2.3 directly addresses these challenges by introducing SDK-powered triggers and actions<sup>4</sup>. This update allows marketers to react instantly to high-intent signals like "add to cart" or "page view" without the typical delays<sup>5</sup>. By enabling immediate and relevant communication, such as abandoned cart reminders, we are not only solving a technical problem but also unlocking one of the most effective e-commerce revenue recovery tactics<sup>6</sup>. This moves MAAC closer to our strategic goal of providing a truly real-time marketing automation platform<sup>7</sup>.

#### Introduction

Journey v2.3: **Real-Time SDK Event Triggers & Retargeting Messages** is a pivotal enhancement that infuses our Journey feature with real-time responsiveness. It introduces two new core capabilities: the ability to trigger and split journeys based on live

**SDK Events** and a new action node to **Send Retargeting Messages**<sup>8</sup>. These features work together to create immediate, behavior-driven experiences that capture customer intent at the most critical moments<sup>99</sup>.

üÜö Optimization for: Real-Time Engagement & Conversion

This update transforms the Journey feature from a scheduled or delayed workflow into a real-time, responsive engine.

| Original Functionality                                     | v2.3 Optimization                                                                                                                                                                        |
| ---------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Journey starts based on tags or delayed GA4 events.        | **SDK Event Triggers:** "Act-in-the-moment" activation based on real-time website behaviors like page views, additions to cart, and purchases<sup>101010</sup>.                          |
| Generic messages are sent regardless of immediate context. | **Send Retargeting Message Node:** Dynamically send messages tailored to a user's specific action, such as reminding them of items left in their cart to drive conversions<sup>11</sup>. |

#### Target Audience & Selling Points

**Primary:** E-commerce Managers, Digital Marketers<sup>12</sup>.

**Personas:**

* **"Conversion-Focused Chloe":** Manages online sales and is obsessed with conversion rates and AOV. Her biggest need is to recover abandoned carts and re-engage hesitant shoppers. She values tools that can react instantly to user behavior to close sales.
* **"Data-Driven David":** Focused on creating highly personalized user experiences based on real-time actions. His biggest need is to move beyond batch-and-blast campaigns and implement true 1:1 communication. He wants to trigger unique flows the second a user shows interest on the website.

**Needs & Pains:**

* **Pain:** Losing sales because abandoned cart reminders are sent too late due to data delays. **Need:** An instant, automated way to re-engage users who abandon their carts<sup>1313</sup>.
* **Pain:** Inability to personalize journeys based on immediate on-site behavior. **Need:** A method to trigger different campaign paths in real-time based on which pages a user visits or what actions they take<sup>14</sup>.

**Selling Points:**

| Feature                      | Pain Point Solved                                                         | Product Feature Value (The Pitch)                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| ---------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **SDK Event Trigger/Split**  | "By the time I know a user has visited a key page, they're already gone." | **Capture Intent Instantly:** "Trigger or split journeys the moment a user views a product, adds to their cart, or makes a purchase. Stop waiting for data to sync and start personalizing their experience in real-time based on their live behavior." <sup>15</sup> |
| **Send Retargeting Message** | "I'm losing too much revenue from abandoned carts every month."           | **Recover Lost Sales Automatically:** "Send a perfectly timed reminder to users who leave items in their cart. Our retargeting node makes it effortless to bring shoppers back to complete their purchase, boosting your conversion rates." <sup>16</sup>             |

#### Combine Feature

* **Real-Time Personalization Flow:** Use the **SDK Event Trigger** to start a journey the moment a user views a specific product page. If they don't add the item to their cart within a set time, use the **Send Retargeting Message** node to send them a message with a special offer for that exact product, creating a powerful, real-time retargeting funnel.

#### Product Value and Differentiation

Our key differentiator is providing a seamless, real-time solution within the MAAC ecosystem that addresses both data latency and permission concerns<sup>17</sup>. While competitors may offer event-based triggers, our native SDK integration ensures the fastest possible response time, moving beyond the limitations of GA4-based actions<sup>18</sup>. This allows for more effective conversion recovery and a more genuinely real-time personalization experience for our clients.

#### Instruction Manual

All features are configured directly within the Journey canvas UI.

* **To configure an SDK Event Trigger:**
  1. In the Journey Builder, select the trigger node.
  2. Choose "SDK Event" as the trigger type<sup>19</sup>.
  3. From the dropdown, select the desired event (page\_view, add\_to\_cart, purchase) to start the journey<sup>20</sup>.
* **To configure a Send Retargeting Message Action:**
  1. Add an action node to your journey canvas.
  2. Select "Send Retargeting Message" as the action type<sup>21</sup>.
  3. Configure the message content within the MAAC message editor, which can include details about the items left in their cart<sup>222222</sup>.

#### Note & FAQ

**Note**

* **Data Source Priority:** If a client has both GA4 and SDK integrations, the SDK event will be the default choice for real-time triggers, though this can be adjusted within the journey settings<sup>23</sup>.
* **Real-Time Execution:** Journeys triggered by SDK events will start for the user in real-time as the action occurs on the website<sup>24</sup>.
* **Message Content:** The retargeting message content is configurable using the standard MAAC message editor<sup>25</sup>.

**FAQ**

* **Q: Why should I use SDK events instead of GA4 events?**
  * **A:** SDK events offer a real-time advantage by firing instantly, which is crucial for time-sensitive actions like abandoned cart reminders<sup>26</sup>. They also provide clients with more direct control over the data shared with MAAC, addressing potential GA4 permission concerns<sup>27</sup>.
* **Q: Can I filter which page views trigger a journey?**
  * **A:** In this version, the trigger is for the general page\_view event. The ability to filter based on specific event properties (like URL) is a future consideration<sup>28</sup>.
* **Q: Can I set a delay on the retargeting message?**
  * **A:** Yes, you can configure delivery conditions such as delaying the message (e.g., "send 2 hours after abandonment") or sending it only during specific time windows<sup>29</sup>.

#### Setting (For CSM)

* **To Enable for a Customer:** The client must have the MAAC SDK implemented on their website. Ensure their plan includes the advanced Journey feature set.
* **Setup Guide:** For a detailed walkthrough on implementing the SDK and setting up the first retargeting journey, please refer to the CSM Technical Playbook: \[Link to CSM Playbook Document].

## Journey v2.X

**Granular Targeting with GA4 Custom Event Triggers** Unlock hyper-specific, behavior-driven journeys by leveraging a wider range of GA4 events, from content engagement to form submissions.

| **PM Owner**            | **Lydia Hou** |
| ----------------------- | ------------- |
| **Product**             | MAAC          |
| **Region**              | All           |
| **Target Release Date** | TBD           |

#### Background

While v2.3 introduced real-time capabilities with the SDK, many clients heavily rely on their existing GA4 setup for comprehensive web analytics. To deepen our integration and unlock more sophisticated marketing scenarios without requiring immediate SDK adoption, this version focuses on expanding our Journey triggers to support a wider range of standard and custom GA4 events. By leveraging detailed GA4 events like scroll depth, form\_submit, and specific click actions, we empower marketers to create highly contextual and behavior-driven journeys. This allows them to react to nuanced user interest signals‚Äîsuch as deep engagement with a page or interaction with specific UI elements‚Äîand to seamlessly connect website form submissions with conversational follow-ups in LINE.

#### Introduction

Journey v2.4: **Granular Targeting with GA4 Custom Event Triggers** moves beyond basic e-commerce events to capture the full spectrum of user engagement signals available in GA4. This update introduces a new suite of trigger and split conditions, allowing marketers to design campaigns that respond to subtle but significant user behaviors.

üÜö **Optimization for: Behavioral Targeting & Deeper Personalization** This update transforms the Journey feature from reacting to broad events to responding to specific, nuanced user interactions.

| **Original Functionality**                                            | **v2.4 Optimization**                                                                                                                                                                     |
| --------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| Journey triggers based on broad e-commerce events (e.g., purchase).   | **GA4 Custom Event Triggers:** "Read-the-intent" activation based on specific behaviors like scroll depth, form submissions, or clicks on particular elements.                            |
| Segmentation is primarily based on user attributes or past purchases. | **Behavior-Driven Segmentation:** Create dynamic segments based on a user's real-time engagement with content and UI elements, identifying interest before a purchase is even considered. |

#### Target Audience & Selling Points

**Primary:** Digital Marketers, Content Marketers, CRM Specialists.

**Personas:**

* **"Content-Focused Carla":** Manages the company blog and resources. Her biggest need is to identify highly engaged readers and nurture them toward conversion. She wants to know who reads articles to the end and which content drives leads.
* **"Data-Driven David":** Focused on creating a seamless omnichannel experience. His biggest need is to connect website interactions (like filling out a form) with immediate, personalized follow-ups in other channels like LINE.

**Needs & Pains:**

* **Pain:** Treating all website visitors the same, unable to distinguish between a casual browser and a highly interested prospect who reads an entire page. **Need:** A way to trigger different journeys based on the depth of content engagement.
* **Pain:** A disconnect between website lead generation (forms) and the communication channel (LINE), causing delayed and impersonal follow-ups. **Need:** A method to instantly trigger a LINE conversation or add a tag the moment a form is submitted.

**Selling Points:**

| **Feature**              | **Pain Point Solved**                                    | **Product Feature Value (The Pitch)**                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| ------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **scroll Depth Trigger** | "I can't tell who's _really_ reading my content."        | **Reward Deep Engagement:** "Identify your most interested prospects by triggering journeys for users who scroll 90% of the way down a page. Nurture their high intent with targeted follow-ups and special offers."  |
| **form\_submit Trigger** | "My follow-up on web form leads is too slow and manual." | **Connect Web Forms to LINE Instantly:** "Turn a static form submission into an immediate conversation. Trigger a personalized welcome journey or a live agent notification on LINE the moment a user hits 'submit'." |
| **click Event Trigger**  | "My website personalization is generic."                 | **Target Based on Precise Interest:** "Launch a tailored journey when a user clicks a specific button or link, like 'Recommendations for 18-25'. Go beyond page views to understand true user intent."                |

#### Combine Feature

* **Content-to-Conversion Funnel:** Use the **scroll** trigger on a blog post to identify engaged readers. Add a **"Highly Engaged" tag** (from v2.2) to these users. If they later visit the pricing page, use the **page\_view** trigger to send a message offering a personalized demo.

#### Product Value and Differentiation

Our key differentiator is moving beyond the standard e-commerce funnel events (add\_to\_cart, purchase). By integrating with a wider array of GA4 events, we empower marketers to engage with customers at every stage of their lifecycle‚Äîfrom initial interest (scroll, click) to lead generation (form\_submit) and retention (session\_start). This provides a much richer, more holistic view of the customer than competitors who focus solely on transactional events.

#### Instruction Manual

Configuration is done directly within the Journey canvas UI.

1. In the Journey Builder, select a Trigger or Split node.
2. Choose "GA4 Event" as the type.
3. A dropdown will now show an expanded list of events, including click, form\_submit, scroll, etc.
4. Select the desired event.
5. Configure the specific parameters for that event (e.g., enter "90" for percent\_scrolled, or the form\_id for a form\_submit).

#### Note & FAQ

**Note**

* **Custom Event Setup:** To use the add\_to\_wishlist trigger, the client must have already implemented this custom event in their own GA4 setup. The feature relies on the client's existing tracking.
* **Parameter-Based Triggering:** The power of these new triggers lies in their parameters. Encourage clients to use specific form\_ids or link\_classes for the most granular control.

**FAQ**

* **Q: Do I need to change my website's GA4 setup to use this?**
  * **A:** For standard events like scroll or page\_view, no changes are needed. To use triggers based on custom events like add\_to\_wishlist or specific form\_ids, you must ensure those events and parameters are being correctly sent to GA4 from your website.
* **Q: How is this different from the v2.3 SDK events?**
  * **A:** SDK events (v2.3) are for **real-time** actions and require separate implementation, making them ideal for time-sensitive triggers like abandoned carts. These GA4 events (v2.4) leverage the rich **analytics data you already have**, allowing for more complex behavioral segmentation, though they are subject to GA4's standard data processing latency.
* **Q: Can I trigger a journey based on a click on&#x20;**_**any**_**&#x20;button?**
  * **A:** You can trigger it based on any click that your GA4 is tracking with identifiable parameters, like a unique link\_url or link\_class. The more specific your GA4 event tracking is, the more targeted your journeys can be.

#### Setting (For CSM)

* **To Enable for a Customer:** This feature is available to all clients with a GA4 integration. No special backend settings are required.
* **Setup Guide:** Proactively ask clients about their key website interactions. Review their GA4 event setup to identify opportunities. Suggest journey ideas based on their existing tracking (e.g., "I see you have a 'Request a Quote' form; let's build a journey to instantly follow up with those leads on LINE.").

üì£ New Feature Release: Trigger now supports ‚ÄúSegment-Based Triggering‚Äù, and nodes now support ‚ÄúAdd and Remove Tag‚Äù actions.

üì£ ‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà: ‡∏ü‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå Trigger ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ‚Äú‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô Journey ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Segment‚Äù ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Node ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ‚Äú‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å‚Äù

### # ÂäüËÉΩÈôêÂà∂ÊèêÈÜí

* ÊØèÂÄãÂ∏≥Êà∂ÊúÄÂ§öÂèØÂêåÊôÇÈÅãË°å 350 ÁµÑÊóÖÁ®ã
* ÊØèÂÄãÊóÖÁ®ãÊúÄÂ§öË®≠ÂÆö 30 ÂÄãÁØÄÈªûÔºàÂåÖÂê´Âá∫Âè£Ôºâ
* **Ë≤ºÊ®ôÁ±§Ëß∏ÁôºÊ¢ù‰ª∂**ÔºöÊØè‰ΩçËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÊØèÂ∞èÊôÇÂÉÖËÉΩËß∏Áôº‰∏ÄÊ¨°
* **GA Ë°åÁÇ∫Ëß∏ÁôºÊ¢ù‰ª∂**ÔºöÊØè‰ΩçËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÊØè 24 Â∞èÊôÇÂÉÖËÉΩËß∏Áôº‰∏ÄÊ¨°
* **ÂàÜÁúæÊõ¥Êñ∞ËàáËß∏ÁôºÊôÇÈñìË™™Êòé**ÔºöÁ≥ªÁµ±Âè™ÊúÉÂú®‰Ω†Ë®≠ÂÆöÁöÑ„Äå**ÊéíÁ®ãËß∏ÁôºÊó•**„ÄçÁï∂Â§©ÂáåÊô®Êõ¥Êñ∞ÂàÜÁúæÂêçÂñÆÔºå‰∏¶ÊñºÊåáÂÆöÊôÇÈñìÊ†πÊìö**Áï∂Êó•Êõ¥Êñ∞ÂæåÁöÑÂàÜÁúæÂêçÂñÆ**ÂïüÂãïÊóÖÁ®ã„ÄÇÂ¶ÇÊûúÊúâËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÊòØÂú®Ë©≤Êó•ÂáåÊô®Êõ¥Êñ∞ÂæåÔºà‰æãÂ¶ÇÊó©‰∏ä 10 ÈªûÔºâÊâçÁ¨¶ÂêàÊ¢ù‰ª∂‰∏¶ÈÄ≤ÂÖ•ÂàÜÁúæÔºå**‰ªñÂÄëÂ∞á‰∏çÊúÉÂèÉËàáÁï∂Â§©ÁöÑÊóÖÁ®ãËß∏Áôº**ÔºåËÄåÊòØË¶ÅÁ≠âÂà∞**‰∏ã‰∏ÄÊ¨°ÊéíÁ®ãÊó•**ÊâçÊúÉÂü∑Ë°å„ÄÇüëâ **ÊèêÈÜíÔºö** ÁÇ∫‰∫ÜËÆìËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ËÉΩÈ†ÜÂà©ÂïüÂãïÊóÖÁ®ãÔºå‰ªñÂÄëÂøÖÈ†à**Âú®ÂàÜÁúæÊõ¥Êñ∞ÂâçÂ∞±Â∑≤Á¨¶ÂêàÊ¢ù‰ª∂‰∏¶Âä†ÂÖ•ÂàÜÁúæ**„ÄÇ
* **Ê®ôÁ±§Êñ∞Â¢ûËàáÁßªÈô§ÈôêÂà∂**ÔºöÊØèÊ¨°Êìç‰ΩúÊúÄÂ§öÂèØÊñ∞Â¢ûÊàñÁßªÈô§ 5 ÂÄãÊ®ôÁ±§ÔºåÁï∂ËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÂêåÊôÇË¢´Ë≤º‰∏äÂ§öÂÄãÊ®ôÁ±§ÔºàÂ¶Ç tagA„ÄÅtagB„ÄÅtagCÔºâÔºåÁ≥ªÁµ±\*\*ÁÑ°Ê≥ï‰øùË≠âË≤ºÊ®ôÈ†ÜÂ∫è„ÄÇ\*\*üëâ **ÊèêÈÜíÔºö** Ëã•ÊúâË≤ºÊ®ôÈ†ÜÂ∫èÈúÄÊ±ÇÔºåÂª∫Ë≠∞Ë™øÊï¥ÊµÅÁ®ãÔºåÈÅøÂÖçÂêåÊôÇË≤º‰∏äÂ§öÂÄãÊ®ôÁ±§„ÄÇ

**Segment Update & Trigger Timing:**

The system updates the segment list at midnight on the scheduled trigger day. The journey will then start at the specified time using the updated segment list from that morning.

If a contact only meets the segment conditions after the midnight update (e.g., at 10:00 AM), they will not be included in that day‚Äôs journey trigger. Instead, they will be included in the next scheduled trigger.

üëâ **Reminder:** To ensure contacts are included in the journey, they must meet the segment criteria **before** the segment is updated at midnight.

**Tag Add/Remove Limitations:**

Each action can add or remove **up to 5 tags** per contact. When applying multiple tags (e.g., tagA, tagB, tagC), the system **does not guarantee the tag order**.

üëâ **Reminder:** If a specific tag order is required, we recommend adjusting your flow to avoid applying multiple tags at once.

üëâ **‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô:** ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Journey ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥ ‡∏û‡∏ß‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå **‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ô**

**‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°/‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å:**

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å **‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î 5 ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á** ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô tagA, tagB, tagC) ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞ **‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ**

üëâ **‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô:** ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏•‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πá‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß

[ÈÅ∏ÊìáËß∏ÁôºÊ¢ù‰ª∂ÔºàÊìá‰∏ÄÔºâ](https://crescendolab.zendesk.com/hc/zh-tw/articles/4413212201113-%E6%95%99%E5%AD%B8-%E8%87%AA%E5%8B%95%E6%97%85%E7%A8%8B-%E5%85%A8%E6%96%B0%E5%8D%87%E7%B4%9A#01JQPFF7W4VPHJYBC0KG9KDJKE)> Êñ∞Â¢ûÂèØÁØ©ÈÅ∏„ÄéTime-based segment Ëß∏ÁôºÊ¢ù‰ª∂„Äè

1. ÈÅ∏ÊìáËß∏ÁôºÊ¢ù‰ª∂ÔºàÊìá‰∏ÄÔºâ ÊØèÂÄãÊóÖÁ®ãÂè™ËÉΩË®≠ÂÆö‰∏ÄÂÄãËß∏Áôº‰æÜÊ∫êÔºåÂèØÈÅ∏È†ÖÁõÆÂ¶Ç‰∏ãÔºö

* Ë≤ºÊ®ôÁ±§Ëß∏ÁôºÔºàÂÉÖËÉΩÈÅ∏Êìá MAAC Êàñ CAAC ‰ªª‰∏Ä‰æÜÊ∫êÔºâ

* **Segment-Based Trigger** (Trigger journey based on segments updated at a fixed interval)
* **‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå** (‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô Journey ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ)

üìå Ë≤ºÊ®ôÁ±§È†ªÁéáÈôêÂà∂ÔºöÂêå‰∏ÄËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÊØèÂ∞èÊôÇÂÉÖËÉΩËß∏Áôº‰∏ÄÊ¨°ÊóÖÁ®ã

üìå GA ‰∫ã‰ª∂Ëß∏ÁôºÈôêÂà∂ÔºöÂêå‰∏ÄËÅØÁµ°‰∫∫ÊØèÊó•ÊúÄÂ§öËß∏Áôº‰∏ÄÊ¨°

üìå **ÂàÜÁúæËß∏ÁôºÈôêÂà∂**Ôºö‰ΩøÁî®ÂàÜÁúæËß∏ÁôºÔºå‰∏ÄÂÆöÈúÄË¶ÅË®≠ÂÆöËß∏ÁôºÈ†ªÁéá„ÄÇÁ≥ªÁµ±Âè™ÊúÉÂú®‰Ω†Ë®≠ÂÆöÁöÑ„Äå**ÊéíÁ®ãËß∏ÁôºÊó•**„ÄçÁï∂Â§©ÂáåÊô®Êõ¥Êñ∞ÂàÜÁúæÂêçÂñÆÔºå‰∏¶ÊñºÊåáÂÆöÊôÇÈñìÊ†πÊìö**Áï∂Êó•Êõ¥Êñ∞ÂæåÁöÑÂàÜÁúæÂêçÂñÆ**ÂïüÂãïÊóÖÁ®ã„ÄÇ

üìå **Segment Trigger Limitation:** When using segment-based triggers, you must set a trigger frequency. The system will update the segment list **at midnight on the scheduled trigger day**, and the journey will start at the specified time based on the updated segment list for that day.

üìå **‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå:** ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå ‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå **‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ** ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô Journey ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ã‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô

**Appendix: User Research- MAAC AI Journey Prototype**

* Context
  * Who are we now?
    * We closed the gap (mostly) from omnichat
    * MAAC = Multi-channel MA tool
  * Where are we heading? ‚Üí AI Omnichannel CEP
    * From Multi-channel to Omnichannel (and more channels)
    * From MA to CEP
    * From non-AI to AI
    * And more trigger types (SDK, CDH, Ëá™ÂÆöÁæ©‰∫ã‰ª∂Ôºâ
  * How will we win?
    * Better: deep LINE integration
    * Different: 2-way comm. (CAAC) compared to MA
    * New: AI, AI, AI
  * In order to support this direction:
